# ep01_prompts — EP01 패널 프롬프트 (54패널 · codex-image)

**확정 일자: 2026-07-12** · prompt-smith
**개정 v2 (화풍 대전환): 2026-07-12** — style-bible v2 §0 갈아끼우기 표대로 54패널 일괄 갱신
입력: `ep01_shotlist.md`(구도·LOC·A/B/C·★SSOT) · `ep01_lettering.md`(말풍선 베이크 명세) · `style-bible.md`(**v2** — 글로벌 스타일·LOC 7종·WARM 토큰·공통 negative) · `character-sheets.md`(불변 토큰) · `refs/INDEX.md`(앵커)
소비자: `_split_prompts.py` → `_render_jobs/panels/` → `_render.sh` · panel-validator · panel-artist-a/b/c

> ## ★★★ v2 화풍 전환 (2026-07-12 · 사용자 판정 "캐릭터와 배경이 따로 논다")
> 바꾼 것은 **그리는 방식뿐이다.** 구도·대사·연기·레퍼런스 앵커는 한 글자도 건드리지 않았다.
>
> | # | 갱신 | 적용 |
> |:-:|---|---|
> | 1 | `STYLE:` 블록 전면 교체 (v1 `HIGHLY DETAILED SEMI-REALISTIC PAINTED ENVIRONMENT` 계열 **전량 삭제** → §1-4 "한 화면 한 손" 블록: 배경도 캐릭터와 **같은 셀 채색·같은 잉크 선**, 가구·소품에 보이는 아웃라인) | **54/54** |
> | 2 | `LOC_*` 7종 전면 교체(§6 재작성본 — 고정 소품=연속성 앵커는 그대로, **묘사만 단순·따뜻하게**) | **52/54** (P53·P54 = 비-공간 엔드카드, LOC 없음) |
> | 3 | ★ `WARM_NIGHT` / `WARM_DAY` 신규 주입(§2-4) | **50/54** — WARM_NIGHT 37 · WARM_DAY 13 |
> | 4 | `negative:` 공통 블록을 §8-5로 교체(사진 렌더링·화풍 불일치·칙칙함 차단 추가). ★ **`no bokeh circles`만 차단하고 소프트 포커스는 허용** — P2/P38 델타 #2(심도 대비) 보존 | **54/54** |
>
> ### ⛔ WARM 토큰 미주입 4패널 (전부 규정에 의한 의도적 예외 — 결손 아님)
> - **P29** `LOC_STAGE` — §2-5 / §8-0 #6의 **유일한 예외**. 무대는 이 작품에서 유일하게 따뜻한 광원이 없는 공간이다(**밝은 곳이 차갑고 어두운 곳이 따뜻하다** = 온도 역전이 회차의 명제).
> - **P2** — §5-B 델타 #3이 **"따뜻한 광원 0"**을 명시(P2=차갑고 P38=따뜻하다는 **온도 반전**이 이 쌍에 준 v2의 선물). 또한 §2-4의 WARM_NIGHT 적용 범위는 **"LOC_BOOTH 내부"**인데 P2는 **유리 바깥에서 들여다보는 카메라**다. → WARM_NIGHT는 P38에만.
>   ※ LOC_BOOTH 토큰 자체의 앰버 악센트는 두 컷 모두에 있다 — P2에선 차가운 글레어가 그것을 덮고, P38에선 글레어가 걷혀 드러난다(§5-B: *"아무것도 추가되지 않았다. 가리고 있던 것이 치워졌을 뿐이다"*).
> - **P53·P54** — 비-공간 엔드카드(`NO scene / NO illustration`). 조명 토큰을 주입하면 모델이 블라인드·목재·천장등을 그리게 되어 카드가 깨진다.
>
> ### 보존 확인 (변경 0)
> 한글 대사 자구(HEAD 대조 **한글 런 87개 전부 동일**) · LETTERING/tail_only/말풍선 0 · ACTING(표정 누출 차단) · REFERENCE ANCHOR · SHOT/COMPOSITION/EMOTION · **`LOCKED_COMPOSITION_P2_P38`(P2·P38 564자 바이트 동일)** · P38 2차 첨부 · P37 물증 명세 · P7 REGEN 보강 · **P22 "만 17세" 판독 예외**(이 패널만 negative에서 `no legible numbers` 제외 — 유지) · scene_group · ratio · refs · output 경로.

> ★ **레퍼런스 이미지 첨부**: 패널별 첨부 시트는 `04_visual/ep01_refs_map.tsv`가 정본이다(렌더 드라이버가 `codex -i`로 첨부).
> 등장하지 않는 캐릭터의 시트는 첨부하지 않는다(종 특징 누출 방지). 캐릭터 0 패널(P22·P53·P54)은 첨부 없음.
> ⛔ 전 패널 negative에 시트 오염 차단(흰 스티커 테두리·순백 배경·다각도 나열) 고정.
> ⛔ `no text` 부정어는 **말풍선 0 패널에만** 쓴다(P38 포함). 대사 패널은 통합 레터링으로 베이크한다.

> ★★ **표정 오버라이드 규약 (2026-07-12 카나리아 후 개정 — 전 패널 적용)**
> 시트를 `-i`로 첨부하면 외형뿐 아니라 **시트의 밝은 카탈로그 표정(활짝 웃음·반짝이는 눈·정면 응시)까지 복사된다**(카나리아 P2·P37·P38 실측).
> ① REFERENCE ANCHOR에 **"시트에서는 디자인만 — 표정·포즈·시선은 복사 금지"** 명시
> ② 매 프롬프트 말미에 **`ACTING (THIS OVERRIDES THE REFERENCE SHEET)`** 블록 — shotlist의 emotion을 **눈매·눈꺼풀·동공·하이라이트·눈썹·부리(입) 모양·고개 각도·시선 방향**까지 구체 묘사(추상어 한 단어로 두면 시트가 이긴다)
> ③ negative에 시트 표정 누출 차단 고정(`do not copy the expression from the reference sheet, no smiling unless specified, no sparkling starry eyes unless specified …`)
> 캐릭터 0 패널(P22·P53·P54)만 예외. **얼굴이 프레임에 없는 패널은 ACTING이 "NO FACE IN FRAME — 얼굴을 그리지 마라"로 명시**된다.

> ★★★ **P2 ↔ P38 구도 잠금 = 이미지 조건화** (텍스트 동일 문자열만으로는 보장 불가 — 카나리아에서 두 컷의 구도가 완전히 달라졌다)
> **panel_038은 첨부 2장**으로 렌더한다: ① `04_visual/refs/Hanji_ref.png` = **캐릭터 디자인** ② `05_panels/ep01/panel_002.png` = **구도 원본**.
> 프롬프트가 두 첨부의 역할을 분리 명시하고, 카메라·인물 크기/배치·배경·프레임을 **그대로 재현**하되 **정확히 3가지(유리 반사광 제거 · 초점이 붐마이크와 입으로 · 색온도/조도)만** 바꾸라고 지시한다. **추가 요소 0**.
> ⚠️ **렌더 순서 의존**: panel_002를 **먼저** 렌더·승인한 뒤 panel_038을 렌더한다(P2를 재렌더하면 P38도 재렌더).

| 그룹 | 패널 | 수 |
|:-:|---|:-:|
| **A** | 001·004·007·010·013·016·019·022·025·028·031·034·037·040·043·046·049·052 | **18** |
| **B** | 002·005·008·011·014·017·020·023·026·029·032·035·038·041·044·047·050·053 | **18** |
| **C** | 003·006·009·012·015·018·021·024·027·030·033·036·039·042·045·048·051·054 | **18** |

---

### panel_001
- scene_group: A
- scene_id: SC01 / location: LOC_BOOTH
- ratio: B
- refs: 04_visual/refs/Hanji_ref.png
- prompt: "STYLE: korean webtoon panel, warm cozy lo-fi anime illustration, ONE UNIFIED DRAWING LANGUAGE for characters AND background - everything in the frame is drawn by the same hand; chibi animal characters (2-3 heads tall) with bold clean black ink outlines, crisp cel shading with one soft gradient pass, large round eyes with bright highlights; the ENVIRONMENT IS DRAWN IN THE SAME CEL-SHADED INK STYLE: simplified rounded props with softened corners, chunky friendly shapes, clean flat color fills, and VISIBLE INK OUTLINES ON ALL FURNITURE AND OBJECTS (slightly thinner than the character outlines but the same black ink); accurate perspective, real esports gear kept recognizable but drawn simply; furniture and peripherals are scaled to the chibi bodies; cozy warm lighting with a warm light source in frame, indigo and violet shadows instead of black, glowing screens with soft bloom; bright saturated colors, inviting cozy atmosphere; NO photographic texture, NO material grain, NO photo lighting; no fantasy elements. ONE single continuous cinematic scene illustration, full-bleed, no panel border, no white margin. . LOC_BOOTH: soundproofed competition booth standing on the arena stage, drawn in warm cel-shaded anime style; egg-crate acoustic foam panels behind the player drawn as a simple repeating diamond pattern with flat fills; a thick glass partition with a few soft hand-drawn smudge shapes (NOT photographic fingerprints); stage lights smeared across that glass as broad flat pale streaks like a water surface; the interior lit by teal-cyan monitor glow with a small warm amber accent light on the desk casting soft orange rim light on the character; the booth interior darkness is deep indigo, never black; rounded boom-mic headset, a generic 5v5 MOBA minimap at the screen edge drawn simply, closed booth door; clean ink outlines on all props, soft bloom, NO lens flare, NO bokeh, NO photo texture . WARM_NIGHT: cozy warm night lighting - the darkness is DEEP INDIGO AND VIOLET, never black; teal-cyan screen glow as the cool key light, PLUS at least one WARM AMBER LIGHT SOURCE visible in frame (a small warm amber accent lamp or warm LED strip on the booth desk) casting soft orange rim light on HANJI and a warm pool of light on the desktop; shadows are saturated indigo-purple, never neutral gray; warm and cool colors meet on every surface; soft glow and gentle bloom around lights; colors stay bright and saturated; low illumination but COZY AND INVITING, absolutely not gloomy or grim . REFERENCE ANCHOR: the attached character reference sheet(s) are the appearance canon - draw the SAME character(s), identical species, fur/plumage colors, eye color, headset color, identifying marks and silhouette. Copy ONLY the character design from the sheet; the sheet's white sticker outline, plain white studio background and multi-view lineup layout must NOT appear - this panel is a single scene inside the environment above. *** DESIGN ONLY - THE SHEET'S FACE IS NOT THIS PANEL'S FACE ***: take from the attached sheet ONLY the DESIGN (species, body proportions, plumage/fur colors, eye color, costume, headset color, identifying marks). The sheet is a catalogue pose - it shows a bright cheerful smile, a wide open happy beak, sparkling starry eyes and a straight-to-camera gaze. THAT EXPRESSION, THAT POSE AND THAT GAZE ARE WRONG FOR THIS PANEL AND MUST NOT BE COPIED. Facial expression, eye shape, eyelid position, pupil size, eye highlights, brow angle, beak/mouth shape, head tilt and gaze direction are defined ONLY by the ACTING block near the end of this prompt, and that ACTING block OVERRIDES the reference sheet wherever the two disagree. . HANJI: chibi penguin, 2-3 heads tall, navy-black head back and flippers, white belly with a soft jagged fur-edge chest ruff, small orange triangular beak, orange webbed feet, ONE dark crown feather with a cream tip standing up from the top of his head, large amber-gold eyes, bright cyan-teal over-ear headset with a dark grey band and a boom mic . SHOT: large establishing wide shot, eye-level medium-long shot taken from INSIDE the booth. COMPOSITION: teammates appear ONLY as dark faceless back-of-head silhouettes lined up left and right; between them HANJI sits on the right third of the frame, STILL WEARING his cyan-teal headset; the closed soundproof door blocks the far right edge of the frame (that closed door is the visual reason there is no crowd noise); the teal-cyan monitor glow is the COOL key light and A SMALL WARM AMBER ACCENT LAMP ON THE BOOTH DESK IS THE SECOND, WARM LIGHT SOURCE IN FRAME - the booth is lit by BOTH; the defeat result on the screen is cropped at a steep angle and blown out so nothing on it can be read. EMOTION: HANJI is motionless, the face of someone whose sound has just been cut off - no tears, no drama, no effect lines. The reading eye travels left to right, out through the closed door. A SMALL WARM AMBER ACCENT LIGHT sits on the booth desk within the frame, and its warm orange rim light catches the edge of HANJI's head and shoulder - he and the room are lit by the SAME light. . ACTING (THIS OVERRIDES THE REFERENCE SHEET - the sheet's cheerful catalogue expression must NOT be copied): HANJI: beak CLOSED in a flat straight line; eyes open but STILL and unfocused, upper lids slightly lowered, ONE small dull highlight per eye and NO sparkles; brows level and slack; gaze aimed straight ahead at the dead screen, NOT at the camera; the face is frozen - the face of someone whose sound has just been cut off. NO smile, NO tears, NO drama. . OUTPUT FORMAT: horizontal 3:2 landscape panel, 1536x1024.. negative: no photorealistic background, no photographic texture, no photo lighting, no realistic office render, no live-action background, no 3d render, no CG background, no photobash, no photograph, no hyperdetailed environment, no material grain, no film grain, no lens flare, no light leaks, no bokeh circles, no chromatic aberration, no HDR, no gritty, no grime, no dirt, no rust, no stains, no scratched surfaces, no macro fingerprints, no mismatched art styles, no character pasted onto a realistic background, no unlined background, no gloomy, no grim, no bleak, no desaturated, no muted colors, no cold gray palette, no clinical office lighting, no black shadows, no pitch black darkness, no watermark, no signature, no artist logo, no brand marks, no english text, no latin letters, no gibberish text, no garbled text, no misspelled korean, no random letters on props, no legible numbers, no digital clock, no timestamps, no scoreboard digits, no real-game UI, no copyrighted champions, no existing game logos, no fantasy, no magic, no system window, no status window, no water, no ocean, no sky, no snow field, no forest, no nest, no spread feathered wings, no flying, no glasses on HANJI, no teal or cyan accents on RAKU's or HOO's props, no tape patch on HOO's headset, no white sticker outline, no die-cut border, no reference sheet layout, no turnaround, no multiple views, no character lineup, no white studio background, no realistic animal anatomy, no crowd faces, no narration box, no character model sheet layout, no plain white background, no speed lines, no focus lines, no sound effect text, no speech bubble, no speech balloon, no balloon tail, no text, no caption, do not copy the expression from the reference sheet, no reference-sheet expression, no catalogue mascot smile, no smiling unless specified, no open happy grin unless specified, no sparkling starry eyes unless specified, no glittering eye sparkles unless specified, no blush unless specified, no raised cheerful eyebrows unless specified, no looking straight at the camera unless specified"
- output: 05_panels/ep01/panel_001.png

### panel_002
- scene_group: B
- scene_id: SC01 / location: LOC_BOOTH
- ratio: A
- refs: 04_visual/refs/Hanji_ref.png
- prompt: "STYLE: korean webtoon panel, warm cozy lo-fi anime illustration, ONE UNIFIED DRAWING LANGUAGE for characters AND background - everything in the frame is drawn by the same hand; chibi animal characters (2-3 heads tall) with bold clean black ink outlines, crisp cel shading with one soft gradient pass, large round eyes with bright highlights; the ENVIRONMENT IS DRAWN IN THE SAME CEL-SHADED INK STYLE: simplified rounded props with softened corners, chunky friendly shapes, clean flat color fills, and VISIBLE INK OUTLINES ON ALL FURNITURE AND OBJECTS (slightly thinner than the character outlines but the same black ink); accurate perspective, real esports gear kept recognizable but drawn simply; furniture and peripherals are scaled to the chibi bodies; cozy warm lighting with a warm light source in frame, indigo and violet shadows instead of black, glowing screens with soft bloom; bright saturated colors, inviting cozy atmosphere; NO photographic texture, NO material grain, NO photo lighting; no fantasy elements. ONE single continuous cinematic scene illustration, full-bleed, no panel border, no white margin. . LOC_BOOTH: soundproofed competition booth standing on the arena stage, drawn in warm cel-shaded anime style; egg-crate acoustic foam panels behind the player drawn as a simple repeating diamond pattern with flat fills; a thick glass partition with a few soft hand-drawn smudge shapes (NOT photographic fingerprints); stage lights smeared across that glass as broad flat pale streaks like a water surface; the interior lit by teal-cyan monitor glow with a small warm amber accent light on the desk casting soft orange rim light on the character; the booth interior darkness is deep indigo, never black; rounded boom-mic headset, a generic 5v5 MOBA minimap at the screen edge drawn simply, closed booth door; clean ink outlines on all props, soft bloom, NO lens flare, NO bokeh, NO photo texture . REFERENCE ANCHOR: the attached character reference sheet(s) are the appearance canon - draw the SAME character(s), identical species, fur/plumage colors, eye color, headset color, identifying marks and silhouette. Copy ONLY the character design from the sheet; the sheet's white sticker outline, plain white studio background and multi-view lineup layout must NOT appear - this panel is a single scene inside the environment above. *** DESIGN ONLY - THE SHEET'S FACE IS NOT THIS PANEL'S FACE ***: take from the attached sheet ONLY the DESIGN (species, body proportions, plumage/fur colors, eye color, costume, headset color, identifying marks). The sheet is a catalogue pose - it shows a bright cheerful smile, a wide open happy beak, sparkling starry eyes and a straight-to-camera gaze. THAT EXPRESSION, THAT POSE AND THAT GAZE ARE WRONG FOR THIS PANEL AND MUST NOT BE COPIED. Facial expression, eye shape, eyelid position, pupil size, eye highlights, brow angle, beak/mouth shape, head tilt and gaze direction are defined ONLY by the ACTING block near the end of this prompt, and that ACTING block OVERRIDES the reference sheet wherever the two disagree. . HANJI: chibi penguin, 2-3 heads tall, navy-black head back and flippers, white belly with a soft jagged fur-edge chest ruff, small orange triangular beak, orange webbed feet, ONE dark crown feather with a cream tip standing up from the top of his head, large amber-gold eyes, bright cyan-teal over-ear headset with a dark grey band and a boom mic . LOCKED_COMPOSITION_P2_P38: camera outside the booth glass looking through it at HANJI inside; HANJI's eye level; three-quarter view turned slightly right of frontal; bust shot (chest up), standard lens, no distortion; HANJI placed slightly LEFT of center, gaze directed toward frame RIGHT (toward his monitor); identical scale, shoulder line at the same height; boom mic in front of his beak at the same angle; identical background: same fingerprint smudge pattern on the glass, same egg-crate acoustic foam panels behind him, same monitor glow position; HIS BEAK IS OPEN - he is mid-speech . P2-SPECIFIC (exactly three deviations, nothing added): (1) the stage lights smear across the glass as a broad reflection that ERASES HALF HIS FACE - HIS OPEN BEAK IS SUBMERGED IN THE GLARE; (2) focus sits on the GLASS SURFACE (reflections and fingerprints are sharp) while HANJI is half soft; (3) cold blue-white stage color temperature with overexposed highlights. EMOTION: unreadable - the glare deletes the expression. FRAMING GUARD: this is a BUST SHOT (chest and shoulders in frame, head occupying roughly the upper half) - do NOT crop in to a face-filling close-up; keep him slightly LEFT of center, keep his monitor glowing at frame RIGHT, and keep his gaze on that monitor, never on the camera. *** MANDATORY GRAPHIC ELEMENT - THE BALLOON TAILS ***: one or two speech-balloon TAILS are drawn inside the booth beside his open beak and they MUST BE CLEARLY VISIBLE - sharp solid triangular spikes, white-filled with a bold black comic-ink outline of the same weight as the linework, unmistakably the pointed tails of speech balloons, aimed down-left into his beak. The balloon BODIES they hang from are drowned in the glass glare, so only a formless blown-out white blur remains where each body would be. DO NOT OMIT THE TAILS - without the tails this panel fails (in the later companion panel the tails are gone and only the open beak remains; that contrast is the point). . SCOPE NOTE: the 'no text' / 'no signage' / 'blank plate' clauses in the environment and character tokens above apply ONLY to signage, plaques, ID cards, screen labels, filenames and props - they DO NOT apply to speech balloons. The speech balloons and Korean hangul specified below MUST be drawn. LETTERING (baked into the artwork): every speech balloon outline and every Korean hangul glyph is hand-lettered into the drawing in the same bold black comic ink as the linework, integrated with the artwork and following the panel's lighting and perspective (NOT a flat typeset/digital-font label pasted on top, NOT a sticker, NOT an overlay); bold gothic sans-serif hangul, pure black, high contrast, horizontal writing, generous padding so no glyph touches the balloon border; every hangul character perfectly legible and correctly spelled. . LETTERING (TAIL-ONLY - the TAILS must be drawn, the LETTERS must not): draw one or two speech-balloon TAILS as SHARP, SOLID, HIGH-CONTRAST shapes - white-filled triangular spikes with a bold black comic-ink outline, the same ink weight as the artwork - sitting just right of HANJI's beak inside the glass and pointing DOWN-LEFT into his open beak. THE TAILS ARE THE WHOLE POINT OF THIS PANEL AND MUST BE UNMISTAKABLY PRESENT AND CRISP. The balloon BODIES the tails hang from are SUBMERGED in the stage-light glare on the glass: only a soft, blown-out, formless white blur remains where each body would be, with no readable outline. There is NO text, NO hangul, NO letters, NO glyphs and NO scribbles anywhere inside or around the balloons or the tails - the reader must SEE that he is speaking and be UNABLE to read what he says. . ACTING (THIS OVERRIDES THE REFERENCE SHEET - the sheet's cheerful catalogue expression must NOT be copied): HANJI: HIS BEAK IS OPEN BECAUSE HE IS TALKING - mid-order, mid-sentence - NOT because he is happy. It is an open SPEAKING beak, not a grin: the beak is parted forward in a call, the corners are not lifted. Brows slightly drawn in, eyes narrowed and hard, pupils small with ONE small dull highlight and NO sparkles; gaze locked on his monitor at FRAME RIGHT - he never looks at the camera. The visible half of the face is tense and unreadable; the glare erases the rest. ABSOLUTELY NO smile, NO cheerful mascot face, NO sparkling eyes. . OUTPUT FORMAT: vertical 2:3 portrait panel, 1024x1536.. negative: no photorealistic background, no photographic texture, no photo lighting, no realistic office render, no live-action background, no 3d render, no CG background, no photobash, no photograph, no hyperdetailed environment, no material grain, no film grain, no lens flare, no light leaks, no bokeh circles, no chromatic aberration, no HDR, no gritty, no grime, no dirt, no rust, no stains, no scratched surfaces, no macro fingerprints, no mismatched art styles, no character pasted onto a realistic background, no unlined background, no gloomy, no grim, no bleak, no desaturated, no muted colors, no cold gray palette, no clinical office lighting, no black shadows, no pitch black darkness, no watermark, no signature, no artist logo, no brand marks, no english text, no latin letters, no gibberish text, no garbled text, no misspelled korean, no random letters on props, no legible numbers, no digital clock, no timestamps, no scoreboard digits, no real-game UI, no copyrighted champions, no existing game logos, no fantasy, no magic, no system window, no status window, no water, no ocean, no sky, no snow field, no forest, no nest, no spread feathered wings, no flying, no glasses on HANJI, no teal or cyan accents on RAKU's or HOO's props, no tape patch on HOO's headset, no white sticker outline, no die-cut border, no reference sheet layout, no turnaround, no multiple views, no character lineup, no white studio background, no realistic animal anatomy, no crowd faces, no narration box, no character model sheet layout, no plain white background, no speed lines, no focus lines, no sound effect text, no text inside the balloon, no letters inside the balloon, no legible words in the balloon, no caption, do not copy the specified, no glittering eye sparkles unless specified, no blush unless specified, no raised cheerful eyebrows unless specified, no looking straight at the camera unless specified, no closed beak, no face-filling close-up crop"
- output: 05_panels/ep01/panel_002.png

### panel_003
- scene_group: C

The flipper must READ AS AN ARM: a rounded shoulder where it enters the frame, a gentle paddle curve, and a blunt rounded tip - NOT a smooth featureless cone or a dark wedge. NO text, NO hangul, NO letters inside the balloons. . HOO (background, slightly soft): a calm READING gaze - eyes steady and level behind the round black glasses, small dark beak CLOSED, brows flat, no warmth, no encouragement, ABSOLUTELY NO smile; he is quietly watching HANJI's back. . He simply holds RAKU's gaze on the level and hands the question straight back - this is the face of someone MEASURING, not welcoming. SHOT: wide medium shot, eye-level - the camera FOLLOWS RAKU. - refs: 04_visual/refs/Hanji_ref.png
- prompt: "STYLE: korean webtoon panel, warm cozy lo-fi anime illustration, ONE UNIFIED DRAWING LANGUAGE for characters AND background - everything in the frame is drawn by the same hand; chibi animal characters (2-3 heads tall) with bold clean black ink outlines, crisp cel shading with one soft gradient pass, large round eyes with bright highlights; the ENVIRONMENT IS DRAWN IN THE SAME CEL-SHADED INK STYLE: simplified rounded props with softened corners, chunky friendly shapes, clean flat color fills, and VISIBLE INK OUTLINES ON ALL FURNITURE AND OBJECTS (slightly thinner than the character outlines but the same black ink); accurate perspective, real esports gear kept recognizable but drawn simply; furniture and peripherals are scaled to the chibi bodies; cozy warm lighting with a warm light source in frame, indigo and violet shadows instead of black, glowing screens with soft bloom; bright saturated colors, inviting cozy atmosphere; NO photographic texture, NO material grain, NO photo lighting; no fantasy elements. ONE single continuous cinematic scene illustration, full-bleed, no panel border, no white margin. . LOC_BOOTH: soundproofed competition booth standing on the arena stage, drawn in warm cel-shaded anime style; egg-crate acoustic foam panels behind the player drawn as a simple repeating diamond pattern with flat fills; a thick glass partition with a few soft hand-drawn smudge shapes (NOT photographic fingerprints); stage lights smeared across that glass as broad flat pale streaks like a water surface; the interior lit by teal-cyan monitor glow with a small warm amber accent light on the desk casting soft orange rim light on the character; the booth interior darkness is deep indigo, never black; rounded boom-mic headset, a generic 5v5 MOBA minimap at the screen edge drawn simply, closed booth door; clean ink outlines on all props, soft bloom, NO lens flare, NO bokeh, NO photo texture . WARM_NIGHT: cozy warm night lighting - the darkness is DEEP INDIGO AND VIOLET, never black; teal-cyan screen glow as the cool key light, PLUS at least one WARM AMBER LIGHT SOURCE visible in frame (desk lamp, warm LED strip, or warm bounce off a surface) casting soft orange rim light on the characters and a warm pool of light on the desktop; shadows are saturated indigo-purple, never neutral gray; warm and cool colors meet on every surface; soft glow and gentle bloom around lights; colors stay bright and saturated; low illumination but COZY AND INVITING, absolutely not gloomy or grim . Copy ONLY the character design from the sheet; the sheet's white sticker outline, plain white studio background and multi-view lineup layout must NOT appear - this panel is a single scene inside the environment above. *** DESIGN ONLY - THE SHEET'S FACE IS NOT THIS PANEL'S FACE ***: take from the attached sheet ONLY the DESIGN (species, body proportions, plumage/fur colors, eye color, costume, headset color, identifying marks). The sheet is a catalogue pose - it shows a bright cheerful smile, a wide open happy beak, sparkling starry eyes and a straight-to-camera gaze. HANJI: chibi penguin, 2-3 heads tall, navy-black head back and flippers, white belly with a soft jagged fur-edge chest ruff, small orange triangular beak, orange webbed feet, ONE dark crown feather with a cream tip standing up from the top of his head, large amber-gold eyes, bright cyan-teal over-ear headset with a dark grey band and a boom mic . SHOT: medium shot, eye-level, from INSIDE the booth (NOT from outside the glass). COMPOSITION: HANJI in profile / three-quarter back view at his station, the generic 5v5 MOBA minimap at the screen edge; two teammate balloons float clipped at the frame edges - and NOTHING comes out of HANJI. The emptiness must be completely un-signposted: no effect lines, no dramatic space, no emphasis of any kind. EMOTION: he simply looks like he is concentrating. . The speech balloons and Korean hangul specified below MUST be drawn. BALLOON 1 (read first), clipped by the UPPER-LEFT frame edge, tail pointing off-frame left, containing EXACTLY the Korean hangul '왼쪽 비었어.' on exactly 1 line. BALLOON 2 (read second), clipped by the UPPER-RIGHT frame edge, tail pointing off-frame right, containing EXACTLY the Korean hangul '야, 들어가?' on exactly 1 line. CRITICAL: HANJI HAS NO SPEECH BALLOON AND NO TAIL - do not draw any balloon, empty balloon, ellipsis balloon or tail anywhere near HANJI, and do not mark the absence with any effect. He is simply silent while his teammates talk. . ACTING (THIS OVERRIDES THE REFERENCE SHEET - the sheet's cheerful catalogue expression must NOT be copied): HANJI is seen from the SIDE / BACK-THREE-QUARTER; what little of the face shows is shut and calm - beak CLOSED, the single visible eye level and fixed on his screen, brows flat, no expression at all. He merely looks 'concentrated'. NO smile, NO sparkles, NO reaction to the teammates' voices, NO turning toward the camera. . SHOT: full-bleed, eye-level, the screen FRONT-ON, with HANJI's boom mic in the near foreground - all three elements below MUST be in this single frame. COMPOSITION: (1) THE SCREEN, filling most of the frame: TWO STACKED WAVEFORM STRIPS, both left-aligned to the SAME starting point on the left. The UPPER strip is CYAN-TEAL (#2FB3A8), DENSELY packed with vertical strokes filling the entire line, and it RUNS ALL THE WAY TO THE RIGHT EDGE of the screen, with small triangular ping markers dotted continuously beneath it. The LOWER strip is drawn in THE EXACT SAME CYAN-TEAL (#2FB3A8) AS THE UPPER STRIP - identical hue, identical saturation, identical glow, same ink. THE ONLY TWO THINGS THAT DIFFER BETWEEN THE TWO STRIPS ARE DENSITY AND LENGTH. The lower strip is almost a FLAT LINE with only two or three short bumps, it BREAKS OFF a little past the halfway point, it has almost NO ping markers, and the rest of its lane is just a dark navy empty groove. *** COLOR IS CRITICAL ***: DO NOT give the lower strip a different color - NOT yellow, NOT amber, NOT orange, NOT white, NOT green, NOT red. Both strips are the SAME cyan-teal. If the two strips are different colors the reader reads them as two different KINDS of data and the whole panel fails - they must read as THE SAME MEASUREMENT taken with THE SAME RULER: one long and dense, one short and flat. A SCRUBBER PLAYHEAD runs VERTICALLY THROUGH BOTH STRIPS AT ONCE (one linked timeline) - this is mandatory, without it the length comparison does not read. (2) HOO's fingertip TAPS THE LOWER, EMPTY STRIP, while his OTHER hand DRAGS THE SCRUBBER BACKWARD. (3) MANDATORY FOREGROUND: HANJI's CYAN-TEAL BOOM MIC - he wears his headset SLUNG AROUND HIS NECK, and that cyan-teal boom mic sits large in the near foreground (lower-left or lower-right corner) in the SAME FRAME as the waveform, so the eye connects the two cyan-teal objects. Nothing is added INSIDE the screen - this link is pure composition. *** B-2 (MANDATORY - the panel fails without it): HANJI'S GAZE IS CAUGHT MID-MOVEMENT, TRAVELLING FROM THE LOWER STRIP UP TO THE UPPER STRIP ***. Draw it unambiguously: his shoulders and body are still squared toward the LOWER strip (the empty one HOO is tapping), his head is only just beginning to TILT UP and his chin is lifting, but HIS EYES HAVE ALREADY ARRIVED - the pupils are rolled UP and sit HIGH against the top of his eyes with the whites showing beneath them, and his line of sight is aimed clearly UP and slightly to the RIGHT, at the dense upper strip and its far right end. The reader must be able to trace the line of his gaze from the empty lower strip up to the full upper one. HE IS NOT LOOKING AT HOO AND NOT LOOKING AT THE CAMERA - he is looking at the upper waveform. FORBIDDEN INSIDE THE SCREEN: no numbers, no time ruler, no timestamps, no counters, no role labels, no filenames, no arrows, no highlight boxes, no circles of emphasis, no comparison captions, no legible letters of any kind (if a ruler is needed, only short unlabeled tick marks). NO cyan or teal on HOO's props. . SCOPE NOTE: the 'no text' / 'no signage' / 'blank plate' clauses in the environment and character tokens above apply ONLY to signage, plaques, ID cards, screen labels, filenames and props - they DO NOT apply to speech balloons. The speech balloons and Korean hangul specified below MUST be drawn. LETTERING (baked into the artwork): every speech balloon outline and every Korean hangul glyph is hand-lettered into the drawing in the same bold black comic ink as the linework, integrated with the artwork and following the panel's lighting and perspective (NOT a flat typeset/digital-font label pasted on top, NOT a sticker, NOT an overlay); bold gothic sans-serif hangul, pure black, high contrast, horizontal writing, generous padding so no glyph touches the balloon border; every hangul character perfectly legible and correctly spelled. . LETTERING: exactly ONE white rounded speech balloon, bold black ink outline, tail pointing up-right toward HOO's beak, containing EXACTLY the Korean hangul '여긴 왜 비었지?' on exactly 1 line, with a clearly drawn question mark. Standard weight - NOT bold, NOT enlarged. PLACEMENT IS CRITICAL: put it in the empty margin ABOVE or at the UPPER-LEFT of the screen so that it and its tail NEVER cover either waveform strip - in particular, the point where the LOWER strip BREAKS OFF and the RIGHT END of the UPPER strip must both remain fully visible. HANJI HAS NO SPEECH BALLOON. This 7-syllable line is the ONLY legible text allowed in the entire panel. . ACTING (THIS OVERRIDES THE REFERENCE SHEET - the sheet's cheerful catalogue expression must NOT be copied): HOO: temperature ZERO - eyes level and steady behind the round black glasses, brows flat, small dark beak parted only enough to ask a short question, body calm; he is MEASURING, not teaching and not cheering. ABSOLUTELY NO smile, NO wide happy open beak, NO sparkling starry eyes, NO warm expression. HANJI: beak CLOSED, brows level, no smile, no sparkles, no tears - ONLY HIS EYES HAVE MOVED (pupils rolled up, as specified in B-2 above). . LOC_DESK: cozy dark analyst room drawn in warm cel-shaded anime style, ceiling lights off; a wall of six simplified rounded monitors glowing teal and cyan is the cool key light, PLUS one warm amber desk lamp in frame casting a warm pool of light on the desk and soft orange rim light on the characters; the darkness is deep indigo and violet, never black; faces lit from below in teal with warm amber on the opposite edge; a replay timeline with a scrubber bar, an enlarged generic 5v5 MOBA minimap, voice-log waveform strips, layers of colorful post-it notes along the monitor bezels, one visibly worn old headset resting on the desk (worn shown by SHAPE - flattened earpads - not by grime), two occupied rounded chairs and ONE EMPTY CHAIR in the corner of the frame, a paper coffee cup, warm wood desktop, a few scattered papers and pens; simplified rounded props with clean black ink outlines and flat cel fills; colors stay bright and saturated; COZY AND WARM, absolutely not gloomy, NO photo texture, NO grime, NO film grain . WARM_NIGHT: cozy warm night lighting - the darkness is DEEP INDIGO AND VIOLET, never black; teal-cyan screen glow as the cool key light, PLUS at least one WARM AMBER LIGHT SOURCE visible in frame (desk lamp, warm LED strip, or warm bounce off a surface) casting soft orange rim light on the characters and a warm pool of light on the desktop; shadows are saturated indigo-purple, never neutral gray; warm and cool colors meet on every surface; soft glow and gentle bloom around lights; colors stay bright and saturated; low illumination but COZY AND INVITING, absolutely not gloomy or grim . Copy ONLY the character design from the sheet; the sheet's white sticker outline, plain white studio background and multi-view lineup layout must NOT appear - this panel is a single scene inside the environment above. *** DESIGN ONLY - THE SHEET'S FACE IS NOT THIS PANEL'S FACE ***: take from the attached sheet ONLY the DESIGN (species, body proportions, plumage/fur colors, eye color, costume, headset color, identifying marks). The sheet is a catalogue pose - it shows a bright cheerful smile, a wide open happy beak, sparkling starry eyes and a straight-to-camera gaze. THAT EXPRESSION, THAT POSE AND THAT GAZE ARE WRONG FOR THIS PANEL AND MUST NOT BE COPIED. Facial expression, eye shape, eyelid position, pupil size, eye highlights, brow angle, beak/mouth shape, head tilt and gaze direction are defined ONLY by the ACTING block near the end of this prompt, and that ACTING block OVERRIDES the reference sheet wherever the two disagree. . RAKU: chibi raccoon, 2-3 heads tall, grey fur, black bandit eye-mask markings over a cream muzzle, cream ear insets, BRIGHT GREEN eyes, small black nose, red over-ear headset with a BEIGE TAPE PATCH on the ear cup and a boom mic, grey hoodie with white drawstrings and a front kangaroo pocket, a black lanyard holding a BLANK white ID card with no text on it, thick black-and-grey ringed bushy tail, dark grey paws . HANJI: chibi penguin, 2-3 heads tall, navy-black head back and flippers, white belly with a soft jagged fur-edge chest ruff, small orange triangular beak, orange webbed feet, ONE dark crown feather with a cream tip standing up from the top of his head, large amber-gold eyes, bright cyan-teal over-ear headset with a dark grey band and a boom mic . HOO: chibi owl, 2-3 heads tall, cream-ivory plumage, brown striped ear tufts, brown-and-cream barred wing feathers, round thin BLACK-RIMMED GLASSES, large amber-gold eyes, small dark grey beak, navy over-ear headset with a boom mic and a small orange chick emblem on the ear cup, an open navy varsity jacket with gold trim and gold pocket welts and a round gold-and-navy circular emblem on the chest, orange-yellow three-toed feet . IDENTITY KEYS (must not mix): HOO wears NAVY headset and is the ONLY one with round black glasses; HANJI wears the CYAN-TEAL headset and has ONE upright crown feather and amber eyes and NO glasses; RAKU wears the RED headset with a beige tape patch and has GREEN eyes, a black bandit mask and a ringed bushy tail. . SHOT: large medium-close shot, eye-level, RAKU frontal and CENTERED. COMPOSITION: RAKU front and center, the face of a flat assertion - brows lowered, eyes hard and still; HANJI is pushed soft to the frame edge; monitor glow lights RAKU from below. The rebuttal arrives straight at the reader. EMOTION: short, painful, and NOT WRONG - absolutely NO malice, NO sneer, NO villainy. . SCOPE NOTE: the 'no text' / 'no signage' / 'blank plate' clauses in the environment and character tokens above apply ONLY to signage, plaques, ID cards, screen labels, filenames and props - they DO NOT apply to speech balloons. The speech balloons and Korean hangul specified below MUST be drawn. LETTERING (baked into the artwork): every speech balloon outline and every Korean hangul glyph is hand-lettered into the drawing in the same bold black comic ink as the linework, integrated with the artwork and following the panel's lighting and perspective (NOT a flat typeset/digital-font label pasted on top, NOT a sticker, NOT an overlay); bold gothic sans-serif hangul, pure black, high contrast, horizontal writing, generous padding so no glyph touches the balloon border; every hangul character perfectly legible and correctly spelled. . LETTERING: exactly ONE white rounded speech balloon, bold black ink outline, triangular tail pointing down to RAKU's mouth, placed in the upper-left margin without covering HANJI's face, containing EXACTLY the Korean hangul '그건 진 사람의 변명이잖아.' on exactly 2 lines: line 1 '그건 진 사람의' / line 2 '변명이잖아.' . ACTING (THIS OVERRIDES THE REFERENCE SHEET - the sheet's cheerful catalogue expression must NOT be copied): RAKU (front medium-close, centered): the face of a FLAT VERDICT - brows LOWERED and set, GREEN eyes hard and steady straight to the front, mouth open on a short blunt sentence. He is not sneering and not gloating - he is being brief, and he is not wrong. NO smirk, NO evil grin, NO cheerful face, NO sparkles. HANJI is pushed to the edge, soft, no readable expression. .
